WAY4™ Upgrade Notes (version 03.48.30)

This document contains upgrade notes of the WAY4™ release [Grouped by Products] or [Grouped by Releases].

To see Check Scripts, click on the [Grouped by Products] link or [Grouped by Releases] link.

Important! These changes may affect your data, please read carefully!

Upgrade Notes on Impact Changes

AMEX interface

CARDS-58930

Renamed Individual Reason Code "4526 Missing signature" to "4526 (old) Missing signature" and marked it as inactive.
Upgrade Note:
Clients who use the AMEX interface should rename the Individual Reason Code for the AMEX channel. Change the code from "4526 Missing signature" to "4526 (old) Missing signature" and set "Is Active" = "No" (OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Transaction Types\Individual Reason Codes).

CARDS-62405

Added MCC 5552 "Electric Vehicle Charging".
Upgrade Note:
Clients who use the AMEX Interface should add MCC "5552 Electric Vehicle Charging" with Group Code "R" and Direct Group "Retail Purchase" (OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Main Tables\SIC Codes).

Accounting

CARDS-60174

Added the "Event Group Code" field to the "Reserve Rates" form (OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Behavior Scoring Setup\Reserving Schemes form -> [Rates]). Now this field's value is not inherited from the "Event Group Code" field of the Reserving Scheme.
Changed the rule of filling in the "Event Group Code" field for the ''Reserve Risk Schemes" form when the [Check] action is applied to the Reserving Scheme.
Upgrade Note:
During the upgrade, the "Event Group Code" field's value for Reserving Schemes can be modified. The "Event Group Code" field will be filled in with the value of the "Group Code" field for an Event type that is set in the "Accrual Code" field for the Reserving Scheme. These changes do not impact the standard Reserving configuration, but may affect some specific and custom solutions. It is recommended to check custom menu items and procedures if they use the "Event Group Code" field of the Reserving Schemes and correct them accordingly.

CARDS-59647

Added the new parameter "FI" to the "com.openwaygroup.pipe.gl.transfers_export.jar" pipe. The pipe will no longer read local constants to define a financial institution or time zone. Financial institution will be taken from pipe parameter. Added the menu item "OpenWay\Time Zone Support\CBS. Outward Processing" with GL export by time zone.
Upgrade Note:
Now the "com.openwaygroup.pipe.gl.transfers_export.jar" pipe accepts a financial institution through pipe parameter, instead of local constants as it was earlier. If custom menu items to call the pipe are used for export by time zones, they must be adapted to transfer FI parameter to pipe.
Updated Manuals: [core_banking_interface\core_banking_interface\administrator_manuals\GL_Transfers_Export.pdf]

CARDS-59937

Added a check that the "Bank Division" field is filled in for bank accounting contracts. If this field is empty, the bank accounting contract approval procedure returns an error.
Upgrade Note:
It is necessary to check bank accounting contracts with an empty "Bank Division" field using the check script CARDS-59937_Empty_Bank_Division.sql. If the result is not empty, set the "Bank Division" field for returned records.
Check Scripts:
CARDS-59937_Empty_Bank_Division.sql

CARDS-60073

Increased size of the returned variable with tagged data from 4000 to 32000 characters in the Balance Prediction functionality.
Upgrade Note:
The signature of the custom procedures CUST_STATE_STR_TO_LOG and CUST_STATE_COLLECT must be changed if these procedures are used in custom procedures/web services.

Acquiring

CARDS-52181

The DCC_CONTRACT tag is checked during Nostro contract approve; it should be the same for Main and Sub Nostro contracts. When searching for the DCC_CONTRACT tag in Nostro contracts, the tag is first searched for in the Sub Nostro contract, then in the Main Nostro contract, and then on the Nostro Account Scheme. Earlier, the DCC_CONTRACT tag value in the Main Nostro contract was not considered.
Upgrade Note:
Clients using Dynamic Currency Conversion (DCC) or Multi Currency Pricing (MCP/MCA) products must perform a check using CHECK_v1_CARDS-52181_dcc_contract_numbers.sql script validating the settings of DCC_CONTRACT tags in NOSTRO contracts. If the check returns a non-empty number of strings, a detailed check must be performed and the results of both checks must be sent to Customer Support.
Updated Manuals: [dcc\DCC_Setup.pdf]

CARDS-60300

Enhanced the opt_acq_payment solution. Supported adding tasks for merchant and partner statement generation on document accept.
Upgrade Note:
The optional ACQ_PAYMENT solution has been changed so that tasks for statement generation can now be created in the CUST_ACCEPT_DOC_AFTER procedure instead of in CUST_ORDER_AMOUNT.
When installing this solution, remove the call of opt_acq_pmnt.ADD_ORDER_TO_STMT_PROCESS from CUST_ORDER_AMOUNT.

CARDS-60656

Optimised memory usage on generation of merchant statement entry detail reports; both standard statements (Merchant Order Entry Details and Merchant Transaction Details) and the optional solution (opt_acq_payment) are affected.
Upgrade Note:
If the optional merchant statement solution (opt_acq_payment) is used, it should be updated to a newer version from the WAY4Card distribution to correspond to changes in the standard acnt_api package.

Acquiring authorisation

CARDS-56042 / I1703295760

Refactored the target contract search algorithm for acquiring and transit authorisations.
Upgrade Note:
It is necessary to check routing contract search scenarios that use the EXCEPTION_BINS parameter or that change the contract in the CUST_DOC_TARGET procedure.
It is also recommended to check the configuration. Run the script CARDS-56042_Check_redef_channel_01.sql and send the result to Customer Support. This information is required for internal analysis of customer configurations for purposes of product development.
Check Scripts:
CARDS-56042_Check_redef_channel_01.sql

CARDS-61176

Changed the behaviour of the CONVERT_ACQ_BIN and CONVERT_ACQ_BIN_CH additional global parameters. The parameters no longer affect transactions received from foreign source channels, i.e. channels with "Is On Us" = "No" in the form "OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Main Tables\Message Channels".
Added the ability to set the parameters CONVERT_ACQ_BIN and CONVERT_ACQ_BIN_CH at the Interchange Routing table level.
Upgrade Note:
If the parameters CONVERT_ACQ_BIN and CONVERT_ACQ_BIN_CH are currently used for transit authorizations from foreign source channels ("Is On Us" = "No" in the form "OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Main Tables\Message Channels"), these parameters should be moved to the interchange routing table. The parameters should be added as tags without values: "CONVERT_ACQ_BIN;" or "CONVERT_ACQ_BIN_CH;" to the "Custom Rules" field of the interchange routing record that is used to define the target contract in the transit transaction.
Updated Manuals: [core\Global_Parameters.pdf]

CARDS-63600

Added checks when changing ATM Cassette Status or changing cassette counters manually using the standard forms "ATM Cassette with Console" (OpenWay\Acquiring\ATM Controller\ATM Monitor - All -> [Cassettes]) and "Cst Console" (OpenWay\Acquiring\ATM Controller\ATM Monitor - All -> [Cassettes] -> [Console]).
Now the "Dispense Parameters" and "Comment Text" fields must not contain a semicolon.
Upgrade Note:
ATM Denominations dictionaries must be checked. If the "Dispense Parameters" field contains a semicolon, it must be replaced by a comma.

TRSW-4149 / I1708083266

Added support for calculating the "NO_AUTH" transaction condition attribute from EMV Data (field 55). The "NO_AUTH" attribute means "Cardholder is not authenticated".
Upgrade Note:
The "NO_AUTH" transaction condition attribute will appear in some documents according to EMV data present in a transaction.

Application management

UFX-497

Changed response message and response file for online and batch UFX Applications for Instalments.
When the parameters "Response=Y" and "AcceptRq=Y" are set in the ResultDtls tag of an online request, the application response for an Instalment application returns instalment brief information (InstalmentRs) in the DataRs section. InstalmentRs includes the following fields:
- InstalmentIDT
- DocID
- Total Amount
- Paid Amount
- Written Off Amount
- Currency
- Status
- dates
This updated behaviour is also applied to batch applications for Instalment management.
Upgrade Note:
Application Response contents have been changed for Instalment applications in online mode and in batch mode. The previous contents of a response (contract data returned) are no longer supported. This should be considered if Instalment applications are already used in the integration layer.
This change affects the following application types (see samples of file applications in manuals\english\application_management\file_samples\issuing\readme.txt):
- Add instalment by transaction                                              
- Update instalment                                                          
- Add instalment                                                             
- Partial EarlyRepayment instalment with KeepInstalmentNumber recalculation  
- Partial EarlyRepayment instalment with KeepInstalmentAmount recalculation  
- Full EarlyRepayment instalment                                             
- PaymentHolidays instalment                                                 
- Close instalment                                                           
New contents of the response message/file:
<DataRs>
  <InstalmentRs>
</DataRs>
Previous contents of the response message/file:
<DataRs>
  <ContractRs>
</DataRs>

CARDS-58532 / I1805035478

Removed client type inheritance from the top level in Application Management R1. 

Previous behaviour: Client type is inherited from the top level. If two clients with different types were created in one application, the error "Client Type modification is not supported in that case" appeared.
If client type was empty, it was inherited from the top level.

New behaviour: Client type is not inherited from the top level.
It is possible to create clients with different client types in one application hierarchy.
If client type is empty, the client will be created with an empty client type.
Upgrade Note:
The old behaviour is no longer supported.
Please check and change, if necessary, the application templates with different values for ClientType contract attributes if these contracts are on different levels of the application hierarchy.

Automated routines

CARDS-56818

Implemented GL closing for a separate financial institution and for a separate Time Zone. The functionality is provided by the "Multiple time zones" license.
Upgrade Note:
The gl.RUN_CLOSE_GL_ORDER procedure signature has been changed, two parameters CloseGLFor and FI have been added. It is necessary to correct custom menu items that call the gl.RUN_CLOSE_GL_ORDER procedure.
Updated Manuals: [accounting\WAY4_Accounting.pdf]

CARDS-58333

Corrected the order in which the "Requested Event Types Check" and "Requested Events Uploading" daily procedures are run in the standard menu "Full → Daily Procedures → Start of Day Step by Step".
Upgrade Note:
In case the "Requested Events Uploading" procedure is run not on a daily basis, as it is recommended, estimate the number of Event types using the "Requested Event Types Check" procedure. If estimation shows a lot of unsynchronised Event types, it is strongly recommended to run the "Requested Events Uploading" procedure when the load on WAY4 is minimum.
Updated Manuals: [automated_routines\Daily_Procedures.pdf]

Case management

CARDS-60452

Changed the structure of the CM_CASE_ACTIV1 index (CM_CASE_ACTIV table). For customizations, including reports that are not supported by OpenWay and select data from the specified table, it is recommended to check the performance of queries with the rebuilt index.
Upgrade Note:
The "Status" field has been added to the CM_CASE_ACTIV1 index of the cm_case_activ table. This can affect custom processes of data export.

CARDS-58257

Fixed delete actions for Case Management Configuration objects (Activity, Strategy, Parm Values, Parameters, Map, Map Scheme).
Upgrade Note:
Clients using the "Case Management" menu item should run a script to check that domain configuration data is correct. If the check returns a non-empty result, send this result to Customer Support for additional instructions.

The "CM.Map" form has been changed. Delete "CM.Map.dataform.xml" from "%OWS_WORK%\client\way4manager\components\dbm.module\dataform" to use the standard form.
Check Scripts:
<OWS Home>\db\scripts\oracle\check\checkdata\cards\CARDS-58257_CM_Conf_check.sql
Updated Manuals: [case_management\Case_Management_Configuration.pdf]

CARDS-59024

Added additional validation of the "Institution" form on the "Approve" action in Case Domain configuration forms.

Configuration inspector

DBK-3890 / I1806039880

Added Configuration Inspector export and import of "Date From", "Date To", "Time From", and "Time To" fields in Event message templates.
Upgrade Note:
When importing Configuration Inspector configuration files that were generated in earlier versions, the error message: "Field <XXXX> not present in source data" will be generated during data merge. To prevent the error, before merging data add the EVNT_MSG_TEMPL table DATE_FROM, DATE_TO, TIME_FROM, and TIME_TO fields with the "Removed" type in the form "Exc Fld Types" (OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Copy Configuration Import\Copy Configuration Import Screen -> [Exc Fld Types]).

Core

CARDS-59705

Changed the behaviour when the "Contract" or "Client" parameter value is cleared. Previously the cleared parameter was present in a client or contract as the tag with an empty value. Now it is removed from client or contract tags.
Upgrade Note:
If there are interfaces/custom code which check contract parameter presence even with empty value - they would be affected. The interface/custom code should be adapted to the new behaviour.
Updated Manuals: [core\Contract_and_Client_Classifiers.pdf]

CARDS-59883

Replaced the standard "RBS. FX Rates Import" pipe with the "com.openwaygroup.pipe.fx_rates_import.jar" pipe.
Upgrade Note:
The standard pipe "RBS. FX Rates Import" has been replaced by the "com.openwaygroup.pipe.fx_rates_import.jar" pipe. The basic logic and format have remained the same, but there are certain differences. 
1. The following pipe parameters became mandatory:
-    SOURCE_DIR (path to the directory with input files).
-    PROCESSED_DIR (path to the directory with successfully processed input files).
-    ERROR_DIR (path to the directory with input files that were processed with errors).
-    OUTPUT_DIR (path to the directory with response files). 
2. The behaviour of the pipe with the parameter FUTURE_RATES_LOADING=N (default value) has been changed. FX Rates from input files are loaded into the FX_RATE table with the "Waiting" status, and then all rates are copied to the FX_SCHEME table. This process involves all "Waiting" rates for the current local date, and not the last rates loaded only.
3. File header format has been changed. The "Inward File Number" field's length has been changed to "2" and the "Reserved" field's length has been changed to "2".
4. The following standard checks have been enabled: 
-    Branch Code from the directory name, file name and file header must be the same.
-    File Creation Date number from the file name and file header must be the same.
-    Row numbers in input files must be in sequential order.
5. Pipe error messages have been rewritten.

Pipe logging level cannot be set with a pipe parameter; instead, use the "Log Level" field in menu item settings.

It is necessary to check and test input files that are used for consistency with new checks.

Every custom menu item that uses the "RBS. FX Rates Import" pipe must be replaced by menu items with the new pipe (Menu Item type: "Special", Special Type: "Java Pipe", Name: "com.openwaygroup.pipe.fx_rates_import.jar"). To do so, use the Menu Item Editor utility. 

For DB Manager users, the CARDS-59883_menu_item_01.sql script is provided to check for use of the "RBS. FX Rates Import" pipe in custom menu items. 

WAY4 Manager users must check whether there are impacted menu items in the "<OW_WORK>\client\way4manager\components\dbm.module\task" folder.
To do so, use the following command:
findstr /M /C:"RBS. FX Rates Import.dll</oref_pipe_name>" *.xml | findstr /C:"name=" /F:/
Every menu item from the "name" field of the command result should be modified to use the new pipe via Menu Item Definition Editor (F7).

If standard menu items with the "RBS. FX Rates Import" pipe were used in Scheduler, they must be replaced by new menu items with the "com.openwaygroup.pipe.fx_rates_import.jar" pipe.
Check Scripts:
Run script CARDS-59883_menu_item_01.sql to check using "RBS. FX Rates Import" pipe in custom menu item. If any records are selected, you should edit menu items to replace call of c-pipe to call of java-pipe "com.openwaygroup.pipe.fx_rates_import.jar".
Updated Manuals: [accounting\Currency_Conversion.pdf] [core_banking_interface\core_banking_interface\administrator_manuals\CBS_FX_Rates.pdf]

CARDS-58131 / I1706150815

Changed the default behaviour for switching on/off additional service packages.
Previously, when an additional service package with a "Default Is Active" field value of "No" was switched on manually for a contract, and then switched off again, this additional service package was permanently switched off. Even if the "Default Is Active" field subsequently changed to "Yes" for the service package. Likewise, when an additional service package with a "Default Is Active" field value of "Yes" was switched off manually for a contract, and then switched on again, this additional service package will be permanently switched on. Even if the "Default Is Active" field subsequently changed to "No" for the service package.
Now, when an additional service package with a "Default Is Active" field value of "No" was switched on manually for a contract, and then switched off again, this additional service package will use the service package's "Default Is Active" field. Therefore, if the "Default Is Active" field of the additional service package is changed to "Yes", it will be "Yes" for the contract. Likewise, when an additional service package with a "Default Is Active" field value of "Yes" was switched off manually for a contract, and then switched on again, this additional service package will use the service package's "Default Is Active" field. Therefore, if the "Default Is Active" field of the additional service package is changed to "No", it will be "No" for the contract.
Upgrade Note:
The configuration of products used in switching on/off additional service packages must be analysed to check if the new system behaviour corresponds to the expected result. In addition, note that now if DEFAULT_IS_ACTIVE = "Y" is set for an additional service package, changes will become effective from the approve date of the main service package (in previous versions, changes became effective immediately).
Updated Manuals: [personal_data_management\Personal_Data_Management_Operational_Manual.pdf] [product_management\Service_Packages.pdf]

CARDS-58087

Fixed Custom Fee processing when both tags FEE_CONTRACT and CONTRACT_FOR are used at the same time.
Upgrade Note:
Run the check script on a test environment prior to the upgrade procedure to find problems in the configuration. If the script result is not zero, configuration must be changed. In this case, contact Customer Support for recommendations on changing the configuration.

UFX-658

Corrected processing of FX rates in the RBS. FX Rates Import pipe when the BANK_DATE_SHIFT parameter is used.
Upgrade Note:
If the BANK_DATE_SHIFT parameter is used in the FX Rates Import pipe to import FX rates for future banking dates, set the parameter FUTURE_RATES_LOADING=Y. Otherwise, FX rates will be loaded for the current local banking date.
Updated Manuals: [core_banking_interface\core_banking_interface\administrator_manuals\CBS_FX_Rates.pdf]

Customer/account management

CARDS-59674

In report Cardholder_Contract_Statement for batch mode added information about top contract in head of report, field named as 
Top Contract # <contract_number>. Also when report generated as XML file in section <G_CLIENT> added two new fields - CLevel as level number of contract tree hierarchy and CTopContract as top contract number
Upgrade Note:
In case the result XML file is loaded to an external system, it is necessary to update the interface in order to match the new format.

CARDS-57867

Changed the algorithm for creating client/contract address lists and logic for transliterating addresses so that addresses are no longer shown multiple times in WAY4 Web screens and in DB Manager/WAY4 Manager forms. See Client Upgrade Notes for additional information.
Upgrade Note:
The algorithm for defining a language for transliterating client or contract addresses has been changed so that addresses are no longer shown multiple times in WAY4 Web address screens and in the "Customer Service Screen" form in DB Manager/WAY4 Manager. 
Previously, to transliterate an address to English, WAY4 used a language specified for the client in case client address was used for the address_type by default (Default Address="Client Base Address" in "ROOT\OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Client Classifiers\Address Types") and there was no address with such address type in the CLIENT_ADDRESS table, 
or in case there was no CLIENT_ADDRESS at all (address was specified only in Client record) . 
The new behaviour is supported by additional global parameter USE_SYSTEM_ADDR_LANG with the "Y" value (default). 
Now WAY4 does not take client language into account, and in the aforementioned case uses the default system language from Global Constants. If language is not set for client or contract address, or it is set to English, or officer language is not defined, no transliteration for this address is performed.
The behaviour can be switched to use client language with additional global parameter USE_SYSTEM_ADDR_LANG set to "N" in case client address was used for the address_type by default and there was no address with such address type in the CLIENT_ADDRESS table, 
or in case there is no CLIENT_ADDRESS at all.

Now the client address list does not contain address specified in client record. The behaviour can be switched to the previous behaviour using additional global parameter USE_CL_BASE_ADDR with the "Y" value.

Logic for generating the list of addresses to show data in the WAY4 Web address screens and in the "Customer Service Screen" form in DB Manager/WAY4 Manager has been fixed:
1. If "Date To" of one address record equals to "Date From" of another address record with the same address type, WAY4 shows the latest created address record.
2. If the activation period of one address record overlaps the activation period of another address record with the same address type, WAY4 shows the address with fewer activation period.
Updated Manuals: [core\Common_References_Books.pdf] [core\Global_Parameters.pdf] [] [issuing\user_manuals\Issuing_Module.pdf]

CARDS-63285

Fixed the "ORA-01403: no data found" error in CSS forms when Last Payment Date was not found.
Upgrade Note:
Changed acnt_api.LATEST_ACTIVITY_DATE behavior - when macrotransaction was not found, NULL values will be returned as Last Payment Amount and Last Payment Date.

Diners Club interface

CARDS-61799 / OWS-6360

Added a new parameter, FIN_TRN_FILTER (instead of FIN_FILTER) to select transactions exported to Diners GV. The FIN_FILTER parameter is used for other selects. Affected pipe: com.openwaygroup.pipe.dci.ipse_standard_data_export.jar.
Upgrade Note:
Clients who use the Diners GV interface must copy the value of the FIN_FILTER parameter to the FIN_TRN_FILTER parameter. The FIN_FILTER parameter must be kept. Conditions in the FIN_FILTER and FIN_TRN_FILTER parameters can be changed independently.

Dispute assistant

CARDS-63578

Added new system activity "Accepted Fraud Report". Now closed cases will not be reopened automatically by accepting a Fraud message for these cases.
Upgrade Note:
Changed default behavior. Previously every incoming safe record matched with a case performs reopening closed case. Now it's an activity configuration option.
Clients who use DA R2 and want to keep previous behavior must set field "Change Case Status" to "To Open" (ROOT\OpenWay\Dispute Assistant R2\Setup\Configuration Setup\Domain Configuration\Activities) for activities: "Accepted Fraud Complaint Confirmation (Iss)", "Accepted Fraud Complaint Reject (Iss)" and "Accepted Fraud Report" (new activity).

Distributed processing

DBK-4894

Fixed an issue with duplicated processes when WAY4 Housekeeping or WAY4 Object Task Scheduler processes were not stopped manually before upgrade.
Upgrade Note:
When upgrading from version 47 and earlier to version 48 and later, all WAY4 Housekeeping and WAY4 Object task scheduler processes must be manually stopped in the WAY4 HA configuration before running upgrade and then restarted after upgrade of each node.

Clients who use Mastercard Fee Prediction and have acquirers in the Europe region must manually add a new tariff type (OpenWay\Tariffs\Tariff Types & Tariff Domains\Tariff Types):
Tariff Role = Service
Name = 'European Commission regulation to cap interchange fee'
Code = MC_EU_CAP
Can Be Personalized by Application = Yes
Tariff Type Group = Null
Default Is Active = Yes

CARDS-60516

Modified Fee Descriptors and Fee Prediction tariffs for transactions in Switzerland according to VISA release item 9.2.5 Apr19-332. Two new values of V_BSA tag (E_CHE and CHE_E) were added with V_FDESC=Default.
Upgrade Note:
Two new values of the V_BSA tag (E_CHE and CHE_E) have been added with V_FDESC=Default. If V_BSA tag values are used to calculate Custom Fees, these two new values should be taken into account.

CARDS-62968

Added Fee Descriptors and Fee Prediction tariffs for Visa consumer transactions originating from EEA countries according to Visa release item "Oct19-524 9.2.3 New Europe Regional Interchange for Visa Consumer Transactions in European Economic Area Countries".
Upgrade Note:

High availability

DBK-4585

Removed check of node availability for all SQL scripts started by OWS Owner.
Upgrade Note:
For High Availability solutions, check third party applications and SQL scripts run by OWS Owner. If possible, run them by another user. Otherwise there will be no check of node availability when changes are made and actions will always be permitted.

DBK-5562

Fixed an issue for clients with "Upgrade Stoplist" flow in a High Availability environment and a version earlier than 03.50.30. In order to successfully upgrade to 03.50.30+, it is mandatory to apply a hotfix on all nodes (si_gen_b.sql package) before upgrade.
Upgrade Note:
Clients with "Upgrade Stoplist" flow and a version earlier than 03.50.30 are affected. In order to successfully upgrade to 03.50.30+, they will need to apply a patch on all nodes (si_gen_b.sql) with this fix before upgrade starts.

Host2Host interface

CARDS-60157

Added message types for transferring messages with the "Cash Dispense (Cardless)" transaction type via H2H clearing channel using the "IC Documents Export" and the "IC Documents Import" pipes.
Upgrade Note:
Customers that process transactions with the  "Cash Dispense (Cardless)" transaction type and use the "IC Documens Import" pipe or "IC Documens Export" pipe should add the following message types using the "OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Transaction Types\Message Types - All" menu item: 
1) "Channel" = "H2H Clearing", "Trans Type" = "Cash Dispense (Cardless)", "Is Authorization" = "Fin", "Category" = "Advice", "Name" = "Cash Dispense (Cardless)", "Code" = "DpP--01-BC" 
2) "Channel" = "H2H Clearing", "Trans Type" = "Cash Dispense (Cardless)", "Is Authorization" = "Fin", "Category" = "Reversal", "Name" = "Cash Dispense (Cardless) Rev", "Code" = "DpR--01-BC" 
3) "Channel" = "H2H Clearing", "Trans Type" = "Cash Dispense (Cardless)", "Is Authorization" = "Fin", "Category" = "Adjustment", "Name" = "Cash Dispense (Cardless) Adj", "Code" = "Dpr--01-BC"
Updated Manuals: [UFX_H2H_Interchange.pdf (NDA Specification for vendors)]

CARDS-59158

Added message types for Note Acceptance transaction type for "H2H Clearing" channel.
Upgrade Note:
Customers who need to process documents with the "Note Acceptance" transaction type via the UFX H2H interface must add the following message types using the "OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Transaction Types\Message Types - All" menu item:
1) "Channel" = "H2H Clearing", "Trans Type" = "Note Acceptance", "Is Authorization" = "Fin", "Category" = "Advice", "Name" = "Note Acceptance", "Code" = "DpP--2X-NA"
2) "Channel" = "H2H Clearing", "Trans Type" = "Note Acceptance", "Is Authorization" = "Fin", "Category" = "Reversal", "Name" = "Note Acceptance Rev", "Code" = "DpR--2X-NA"
3) "Channel" = "H2H Clearing", "Trans Type" = "Note Acceptance", "Is Authorization" = "Fin", "Category" = "Adjustment", "Name" = "Note Acceptance Adj", "Code" = "Dpr--2X-NA"
Updated Manuals: [UFX_H2H_Interchange.pdf (NDA Specification for vendors)]

CARDS-64402

Corrected transaction condition attributes for credential-on-file transactions. Now if a transaction has the "STORED" transaction attribute, the "KEY_ENTRY" transaction attribute will be removed.
Upgrade Note:
The change impacts transaction conditions for transit, issuing and acquiring transactions. So it affects services, usage limiters, tariffs definition. It is recommended to check authorization scenarios.

Housekeeping

DBK-4841

FIxed an issue when WAY4 Housekeeping failed with the exception ORA-01917: user or role does not exist.
Upgrade Note:
If "lazy sys" functionality is used during upgrade of WAY4 Cards (Upgrade.lazysys=Y setting in the db.ini file), it is necessary to recreate Housekeeping objects. This procedure is described in the standard document "Creating an Owner of WAY4™ Housekeeping Archive Tables".

Instalment management

CARDS-57816

Added the ability to convert an authorisation to instalment from the "Auth" link in the "Instalment Contract Data" form. An instalment plan status is set according to the INST_APPROVE_PLANS parameter. 
If INST_APPROVE_PLANS=Y, the plan is assigned the "Preview" status. After approval or if INST_APPROVE_PLANS=N the plan status becomes "Inactive" and awaits of financial document posting. After a financial document has been posted, the instalment plan is activated or recalculated according to the INST_FIN_ACTION parameter. New custom function CUST_INSTL_ACTION is called during financial document posting that makes it possible to define what to do with the instalment plan if some attributes of the financial document differ from the authorisation.
Upgrade Note:
The behaviour of instalment plan activation in the "Preview" status has been changed during financial document posting. If the parameter INST_APPROVE_PLANS=Y is configured, an instalment plan in the "Preview" status linked to an authorisation document will not be approved. The plan will be just relinked to the financial document and will require manual approval.
Updated Manuals: [instalment_management\WAY4_Instalments.pdf]

CARDS-59876

Changed value format of the INST_IRATE and INST_IRATE_FREE tags. Now the value must be specified with the decimal separator ".". Previously the value was specified in ISO format without decimal separator. Now all instalment-related tags specifiing interest and fee rates will have the same format.
Upgrade Note:
To use a new value format (with the decimal separator "."), a custom code that sets the INST_IRATE and INST_IRATE_FREE tags in documents must be corrected .
Updated Manuals: [instalment_management\WAY4_Instalments.pdf]

CARDS-62601

Extended instalment creation/activation when a financial document is processed if the ACTIVATE_RECALC instalment action is configured. Instalment parameters from the financial document will be compared with an authorisation document. If the same parameters are used and no portions of instalment plan created on authorisation became open, an instalment plan from authorisation will be activated, a new plan will not be created. If some parameters are different or no instalment plan found for authorisation (or there is no authorisation), a new instalment plan will be created.
If contract parameters changed since authorisation and no instalment scheme is found for a new plan creation, an instalment scheme from the authorisation plan will be used not checking scheme parameters.
Upgrade Note:
If the INST_FIN_ACTION=ACTIVATE_RECALC mode is used, Invoice Events reconfiguration is required. To activate funds transfer, add records with Action = Activate. For example, if INST_AUTH_ACTION=CREATE_INACTIVE, records with Action = Activate, and Status Before = INACTIVE, and Status After = ACTIVE must be added.

CARDS-58785

Changed the instalment functional dates calculation algorithm (Instalment Effective Date, Instalment Due Date, and Instalment Report Date). The "PAYMENT_DUE_ADVANCE" and "DUE_TO_WRK_DAY" parameters that are set globally or on Account Scheme level are no longer used.
Upgrade Note:
To check whether the change affected functional dates in the system configuration, run the check script "CARDS-58785_instl_date_schemes_01.sql".
Check Scripts:
CARDS-58785_instl_date_schemes_01.sql

CARDS-62259

Added the restriction on a new instalment scheme for the "Change Instalment Terms" action. The new scheme must have the same "Invoice Code" as the current scheme.
To enable the selection of an instalment scheme with the different invoice code, the INST_ALLOW_CODE_CHANGE global parameter should be set to "Y" (can be redefined in financial institution). The default parameter value is "N", that is the invoice code cannot be changed.
Upgrade Note:
The default behaviour of the "Change Instalment Terms" action has been changed. Now selecting an instalment scheme with the invoice code different from that of the current instalment plan scheme is restricted by default. To enable the old behaviour, the INST_ALLOW_CODE_CHANGE global parameter must be set to "Y" (can be redefined in financial institution).
Note that if changing invoice code is enabled, invoice Events and standing payment orders to transfer funds to appropriate accounts must be configured.
Updated Manuals: [instalment_management\WAY4_Instalments.pdf]

Issuing

CARDS-61043

Fixed the default classifier value assigned to a new card contract after reissuing with the same product and the SKIP_FOR_DUPLICATE classifier attribute. Correct behaviour - the classifier value for the new card should be taken from the default value defined for the Product, not the general default value for this classifier.
Upgrade Note:
The CARDS-61043_product_classifier.sql script is used to detect a problematic configuration in which a classifier with SetToContract = Yes or null and the SKIP_FOR_DUPLICATE tag is set for the product. After running the script, check the Process Log for a process named "Checking product options with SKIP_FOR_DUPLICATE". If there are any Warnings in process messages, note that behaviour when a card is reissued with the same product might be changed due to this fix. If the new behaviour does not correspond to expectations, contact Customer Support with a detailed description of the required behaviour.
Check Scripts:
CARDS-61043_product_classifier.sql
Updated Manuals: [issuing\user_manuals\Issuing_Module.pdf]

CARDS-61244

Fixed an issue with duplication of the blocked amount under the main contract when a card is reissued with a new PAN and the "Check" or "Billing Limit" authorisation scenario.
Upgrade Note:
It is recommended to check the performance of the process for reissuing lost or stolen cards that have the "Check" or "Billing Limit" authorisation scenario.

Issuing authorisation

CARDS-59236

Changed the algorithm for calculation of the fee amount for blocking on Issuing authorization. The target fee amount from the authorization document is used now as the fee amount of the main service. If it is absent, it will be recalculated according to the Target Service configuration. Previously, it was always recalculated, even if the document already had Fee Amount information. These changes do not impact standard Issuing Authorization, as it does not have any predefined Fee Amounts, but may affect some specific and custom solutions.
Upgrade Note:
It is necessary to check if configurations exist in which the actual fee amount that is specified in a document's "Target Fee Amount" field is blocked for the contract according to a custom fee under the main Service. The custom fee has the field value "Fee Percentage" = 100% and "<AUTH>" and "TGTFD" tags in the "Service Details" field. To check for problematic configurations, use the check script CARDS-59236_DOC_FEE_AMOUNT_01.sql.
If problems are found, contact Customer Support.
Check Scripts:
CARDS-59236_DOC_FEE_AMOUNT_01.sql

CARDS-60053

Redesigned the algorithm for additional authorisation limit processing (hardcoded tariff OVL_THRESHOLD) - now it is checked during calculation of the amount available.
Upgrade Note:
It is highly recommended to carefully test the functionality for hidden additional authorisation limits.
Updated Manuals: [issuing\user_manuals\Issuing_Module.pdf] [tariff_management\Tariff_Management.pdf]

TRSW-4622

Replaced the Thales HSM "NC" command with the more suitable "NO" in nettest and keepAlive commands on HSMThalesAdapter. Enabled by default for Thales 9000. To enable the previous behaviour, set usePerformDiagnosticsForNettest="true" in HSMAdapter.s.xml.
Upgrade Note:
Contact Customer Support if WAY4 Transaction Switch functionality is used that requires special permissions or license file.

TRSW-4635

Started to send scheme name for EPIN and DIN processing from TS to AuthServer if it was provided in card_parms.
Upgrade Note:
Default authType values in call to AuthServer have been changed ("EPIN" instead of "EPIN_AUTH" and "OTP_MMA" instead of "VDIN"). If previous values were used, configuration of AuthServer should be changed or a value configured in Cards to be returned in the EPIN/DIN tag on GetCardParms according to changes made in linked CARDS-57547 issue.

CARDS-61948 / OWS-10097

Changed the algorithm of plastic record selection for non-chip transactions. When there are locked and unlocked plastics with an expiry date that correspond to the request's data, the record for the unlocked plastic will be selected.
Upgrade Note:
It is necessary to check authorization scenarios for the cards reissued with the same expiration date.
Updated Manuals: [issuing_authorisation\Authorisation_system.pdf]

CARDS-63617 / OWS-14239

Corrected the algorithm for generating an issuing authorization response code to eliminate the possibility that the response code value stored in the document record will be changed incorrectly.
Upgrade Note:
Before this change it was possible to amend RC code for completed authorization requests if the code value was greater than 99. This approach is discontinued now. Please check your business processes to ensure that this modification does not affect them.

CARDS-61709

Fixed an issue with authorisation from a special balance type: now the credit history is set for a contract's specific balance and affects the balance's available value. This issue appeared when the the target service account was not included in the balance type which was set in the service (for example if a service balance type was used).
Upgrade Note:
To find a configuration which might be affected by the changes, run the check script CARDS-61709_bt_rule.sql. If the script returns any value, please contact Support.

MasterCard interface

CARDS-57515

Changed the default value of the "MC_PRC_TA" global parameter from "N" to "Y". This parameter manages if transaction attributes are calculated by special DB procedures ('Y" value) or by MC clearing pipes. Pipes affected: "IPM Outward Processing.dll", "IPM Inward Processing.dll"
Upgrade Note:
To restore the old behaviour, the "MC_PRC_TA" global parameter must be set to the "N" value.
Updated Manuals: [core\Global_Parameters.pdf]

CARDS-58481

Added the ability to customise file names for the "MABU Acquirer Merchant Registration Requests Export" and "MABU Acquirer Requests Export" pipes.
Upgrade Note:
Added the "FILE_NAME_PREFIX" pipe parameter which allows the prefix of an exported file to be modified. For the "MABU Acquirer Merchant Registration Requests Export" pipe, the parameter's default value is "MABU_AMR_"; for the "MABU Acquirer Requests Export" pipe, the parameter's default value is "MABU_AER_". The default file name for the "MABU Acquirer Requests Export" and "MABU Acquirer Merchant Registration Requests Export" pipes has been changed. To restore previous behaviour, the "FILE_NAME_PREFIX"="MABU_" pipe parameter must be set for the "MABU Acquirer Requests Export" pipe and "FILE_NAME_PREFIX"="MABU_MERCH_" for the "MABU Acquirer Merchant Registration Requests Export" pipe.
Updated Manuals: [abu_acquiring\mastercard_automatic_billing_updater\Interacting_with_MABU_Acquiring.pdf]

CARDS-59060

Added the ability to change IRD for secondary dispute transactions when exporting to Mastercard with the "IPM Outward Processing" pipe.
Upgrade Note:
To override IRD for secondary dispute documents when exporting transactions to Mastercard with the "IPM Outward Processing", the appropriate IRD value must be put in the "doc.target_fee_code" database field. This can be helpful in some emergency cases when the previous incoming transaction from Mastercard has an incorrect IRD.

CARDS-60250

Added the ability in the "MABU Issuer Request Export" pipe to set different endpoint numbers for different ICAs when exporting file using file names according "Mastercard Global File Transfer System" format .
Upgrade Note:
To set different endpoint numbers in file name for different ICAs when exporting file by the "MABU Issuer Request Export" pipe using file name format according "Mastercard Global File Transfer System"  (the "FILE_NAME_FMT"="GFT" pipe parameter is set) the new "ICA_ENDPOINTS" pipe parameter must be used.
Format for this parameter is <ica1>:<endpoint1>,<ica2>:<endpoint2>,...<icaN>:<endpointN>, where <endpointN> is endpoint number for ICA <icaN>.
Updated Manuals: [abu_issuing\mastercard_automatic_billing_updater\Interacting_with_MABU_Issuing.pdf]

CARDS-54612

Enhanced calculation for "Number Of Issued Chip Cards", "of which are only Contact", "of which are Contact and Contactless", "of which are only Contactless", "of which are micro tags", "Number Of Active Cards (at least one transaction)", "Number Of Active Cards (at least one Contactless transaction)", "Number of Accounts", and "Number of Active Accounts" fields in the "Card Issuance" section of the "Visa Statistics Issuing Business" report.
Now only contracts/accounts with valid statuses are included in calculations of the values listed above. Contract status history can be taken into account. 

For the "Accounts and Cards" section of the"MC Statistics Issuing Business" report:
Enhanced calculation for the "Accounts at beginning of quarter" (Open/Blocked/Total), "Accounts at end of quarter" (Open/Blocked/Total), "Cards at beginning of quarter" (Open/Blocked/Total), and "Cards at end of quarter" (Open/Blocked/Total) fields. Now the values listed above are calculated based on contract/account status validity where contract status history can be taken into account.
Renamed the "Of which are MasterCard contactless" field to "Of which are MasterCard contactless enabled".
Corrected calculation for "Total MasterCard contactless Cards issued". Now all valid cards enabled to perform contactless transactions are calculated; previously only active cards were calculated.
Upgrade Note:
Only the new calculation algorithm is available for the fields of the "Card Issuance" section of the "Visa Statistics Issuing Business" report and the "Accounting and Cards" section of the "MC Statistics Issuing Business" report.
Old behaviour is not supported.
Current values for the aforementioned sections can differ from the previous ones since an additional condition for cards/accounts to have proper statuses has been added.
To use historical values of contract statuses (values for reporting dates), create a standard contract "CONTR_STATUS" classifier. Otherwise the current contract status value will be used.
Updated Manuals: [mastercard_statistical_reports\quarterly_mastercard_reporting\MC_Statistical_Reports.pdf] [visa_statistical_reports\quarterly_operating_certificates\VISA_Statistical_Reports.pdf]

CARDS-59322

Added the ability in the "MABU Issuer Request Export" pipe to generate the name of an exported file in "Mastercard Global File Transfer System" format .
Upgrade Note:
To set the name of a file that is exported by the "MABU Issuer Request Export" pipe according to the "Mastercard Global File Transfer System" naming convention, set the new pipe parameter "FILE_NAME_FMT"="GFT". It is also necessary to set the new pipe parameter "FILE_NAME_PREFIX". The "FILE_NAME_PREFIX" pipe parameter value must contain the part of the  file name before the date time part (for example "MCI.AR.R274.C.E0023456", see Mastercard "File Transfer Manual" manual, chapter "File Naming Convention in the Mastercard Repository" for values).
Updated Manuals: [abu_issuing\mastercard_automatic_billing_updater\Interacting_with_MABU_Issuing.pdf]

CARDS-59521

Supported import of Mastercard "Issuer Account Change Confirmation" files with information for several ICAs by the "MABU Issuer Response Import" pipe.
Upgrade Note:
If the "Issuer Account Change Confirmation" file contains information not only for "our" ICA, but also for external ICAs (i.e. for affiliates), the new pipe parameter "OUR_ICA_LIST" must be set. The parameter's value must contain "our" ICAs delimited by commas. In this case, infomation for ICAs not listed in the parameter will be exported in a separate file in the directory, defined in the new pipe parameter "OUTPUT_DIRECTORY".
Updated Manuals: [abu_issuing\mastercard_automatic_billing_updater\Interacting_with_MABU_Issuing.pdf]

CARDS-60894

Fixed an issue when field DE22.4 of a clearing file exported by the "IPM Outward Processing" pipe had an incorrect value for the first recurring transaction.
Upgrade Note:
To switch the system to the new behaviour, the following changes should be made: 
1. If the online Mastercard interface is on Transaction Switch, check that Transaction Switch contains TRSW-5683. Make changes according to Upgrade Notes for TRSW-5683. 
2. If the online Mastercard interface is on NetServer, changes will automatically take place on April 12.
3. In the "IPS Release Changes" form (Full -> Configuration Setup -> Main Tables -> IPS Release Changes), add a record with the following values: 
Payment System = MasterCard 
Target = Clearing
Release Number = 19Q2 
Article Number = Edit21 
Date From = Proper date from: the same as set for Target = "Online" or April 12

CARDS-59336 / I1808153593

Changed default menu items for importing and exporting transactions to NSPK in Mastercard IPM format according to NSPK operational bulletin #43.2018.
Upgrade Note:
Clients in Russia that process Mastercard transactions should review menu items for importing and exporting these transactions to NSPK.

Inward Processing: if the "FILE_FORMAT" pipe parameter in the menu item for importing IPM files is absent or has the value "U1014", additional actions are not required. If "FILE_FORMAT" has the "RDW" value, it should be deleted before the first import of a file in 1014 blocked format.

Outward Processing: if the "FILE_FORMAT" pipe parameter in menu items for exporting IPM files (including Collection only files) is absent or has the value "U1014", additional actions are not required. If "FILE_FORMAT" has the "RDW" value, it should be deleted before the first export of a file in 1014 blocked format. Also if the menu item has a subitem for conversion from RDW to 1014 blocked format, this subitem shoud be deleted and the "IPMMAST__INITIAL_DIR" pipe parameter must be reviewed. It should contain the final (not temporary) directory.

Note that exported files must be sent to Mastercard also (not only to NSPK) according to "Mastercard Bulletin No.4 3 May 2016" as earlier. Since now NSPK and Mastercard formats match each other, there is no need to generate 2 files. A copy of the NSPK file can be sent to Mastercard.

CARDS-59098

Changed processing of NSPK MIR dispute transactions. Additional setup is required before upgrade, see Client Upgrade Notes for details.
Upgrade Note:
MIR members and affiliate banks that use the WAY4 platform with UFX Host-to-Host interchange, before upgrading WAY4 Cards to version 03.48.30.00 and later must configure new transaction types for "Adjustment" messages.

The mechanism for generating and processing in WAY4 incoming "Adjustment" dispute messages from MIR has changed. Documents for this type of message are generated as secondary transactions with a new chain type, Dispute Resolution, and new transaction types:
* Dispute Resolution Debit (debit the account of the bank that received the "Adjustment" message, according to the result of the dispute cycle) 
* Dispute Resolution Credit (credit the account of the bank that received the "Adjustment" message, according to the result of the dispute cycle). 

File exchange of documents for "Adjustment" messages between a MIR member (sponsor) and affiliate banks is supported exclusively through UFX Host-to-Host interchange. The appropriate changes have been made to the inter-vendor specification on UFX Host-to-Host interchange.

Contact Customer Support for instructions.

Product management

CARDS-58811

Added a new value type for Contract Parameters, "Date".
Implemented the ability to use a Contract Parameter with the "Date" value type as the base date for charging Weekly/Monthly/Quarterly/Yearly fees.
A weekly fee will be charged every week on the same day starting from the base date that is defined by the corresponding Contract Parameter.
A monthly fee will be charged every month on the same day starting from the base date that is defined by the corresponding Contract Parameter.
A quarterly fee will be charged every 3 months on the same day starting from the base date.
A yearly fee will be charged every year on the same day according to the base date. The start date of a Yearly fee also depends on Fee Day.
Upgrade Note:
Previously, the BASE_DATE tag specified in transaction subtypes and in standing payment orders activated with "Weekly", "Monthly" and "Quarterly" frequency was ignored in standard calculation of frequency. Now the value of the BASE_DATE tag is used in calculation for fees that are charged with a "Weekly", "Monthly" and "Quarterly" frequency, and for recurring standing payment orders that are activated with this frequency. If the BASE_DATE tag is set for a transaction subtype or standing payment order, the Value Days value of a Service or standing payment order is ignored. Therefore, it is necessary to check for transaction subtypes and standing payment orders that have "Weekly", "Monthly" and "Quarterly" frequency of activation with the BASE_DATE tag using the check scripts CARDS-58811_BASE_DATE_01.sql and CARDS-58811_BASE_DATE_02.sql, respectively. When this configuration is present, ensure that this tag is not used in custom code and clear it. Or, if this tag is used in custom setup, change the custom code and rename the tag.
Check Scripts:
CARDS-58811_BASE_DATE_01.sql, CARDS-58811_BASE_DATE_02.sql
Updated Manuals: [core\Contract_and_Client_Classifiers.pdf] [product_management\Service_Packages.pdf] [product_management\Standing_Orders.pdf] [core\Setup_Tags.pdf]

CARDS-61494

Corrected the CLOSE_IF_EMPTY%-statement processing: registration in balance type table is mandatory for user balance types and is not required for hardcoded balance types.

Use the script CARDS-61494_event_type.sql to find balance types which are not registered in the system (including hardcoded balance types) but are specified in the tags "CLOSE_IF EMPTY" and "CLOSE_IF EMPTY_LIAB" for Events. Analyse the records returned by the script and change settings, if necessary:
- Custom balance types must be registered in the "Balance Type" dictionary if they must be checked when closing an Event; otherwise, they must be excluded from Event type settings.
- For hardcoded balances, system behaviour has changed: now balance types will always be checked when processing the corresponding Events (hardcoded balance types do not have to be registered in the "Balance Type" dictionary). Previously, if hardcoded balance types were not registered in the the "Balance Type" dictionary, they were not checked when closing an Event.

- Custom balance types must be registered in the "Balance Type" dictionary if they must be checked when closing an Event; otherwise, they must be excluded from Event type settings.
- For hardcoded balances, system behaviour has changed: now balance types will always be checked when processing the corresponding Events (hardcoded balance types do not have to be registered in the "Balance Type" dictionary). Previously, if hardcoded balance types were not registered in the the "Balance Type" dictionary, they were not checked when closing an Event.

CARDS-65146

Fixed incorrect MTP calculation with the BT_SIMPLE algorithm when the PAST_DUE balance is more than the MTP_AGED_PART amount.
Upgrade Note:
1. The script CARDS--65146_BALANCE_TYPE.sql checks a configuration for a MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV balance, which is used to calculate the minimum payment (MTP) according to the BT_SIMPLE algorithm. If the script result is not empty - note that rules for calculating MTP according to the BT_SIMPLE-PAST_DUE[-OVL] formula have been changed.
Old behavior:
CurrentDue = rate*(MTP_AGED_PART-PAST_DUE[-OVL])+MTP_AGED_FULL
New Behavior:
CurrentDue = rate*(MTP_AGED_PART-PAST_DUE+MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV[-OVL])+MTP_AGED_FULL
The reason for the change is that a MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV balance is part of a PAST_DUE balance and the previous behavior was found to be incorrect.
If the MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV balance is used in the configuration, this balance's setup must be checked. This balance type should be defined for the account template that is specified as the Due Template for the account template with the MTP_AGED_FULL balance.
Example:
A line of accounts is configured in an Account Scheme:
Fee Current->Fee Grace->Fee Billed
A fee is included in MTP as 100%. The Fee Grace account should be marked with the MTP_AGED_FULL balance. The Fee Billed account template must be marked with the MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV balance.
2. The script CARDS--65146_ACC_SCHEMES.sql checks the configuration for the mode for calculating MTP according to BT_SIMPLE-PAST_DUE [-OVL]. If this mode is used and there are also account templates marked with the MTP_AGED_FULL balance (i.e. included in MTP as 100%), it is recommended to switch to the new mode for calculation according to the following formula:
CurrentDue = rate*(MTP_AGED_PART-PAST_DUE+MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV-[OVL])+MTP_AGED_FULL
where MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV is the balance that was already (in previous cycles) included in MTP as 100% according to the MTP_AGED_FULL balance but has not been paid yet.
The following changes should be made to the configuration:
1) Create a new balance type MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV in the form "OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Accounting Setup\Balance Types" with the parameters:
Code = MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV
Main Only=Main Only
History Mode = None
2) For account templates which are defined as Due templates for the account templates marked with MTP_AGED_FULL balance - add the value MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV to the Extra Bal Type field.
Example:
The following account templates and ageing rule for them are defined in the account scheme:
Fee Current->Fee Grace->Fee Billed
The fee is included in MTP as 100%. In the current configuration, the Fee Grace account template is marked with the MTP_AGED_FULL balance. The Fee Billed account template is not marked with the MTP_AGED_FULL balance. In this case, this account template should be marked with MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV balance.
3) Recalculate the MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV balance for existing contracts by using "OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Accounting Setup\Balance Types"->Recalc Balance For All Contracts.
Check Scripts:
CARDS--65146_BALANCE_TYPE.sql
CARDS--65146_ACC_SCHEMES.sql

CARDS-56635 / I1712085785

Changed the default behaviour of Events duplication when Contract is duplicated (reissued, etc.). Events with the "Waiting" status are now duplicated to a new contract along with Events with the "Posted", "Suspended", and "Inactive" statuses. Sometimes, Events with the "Waiting" status must not be duplicated to a new contract, for example, if they relate to the previous contract closing. These Events must be marked with the SKIP_FOR_DUPLICATE; tag.
Upgrade Note:
Event types that are used for reissuing card contracts and must not be duplicated to a newly created contract must be checked. The SKIP_FOR_DUPLICATE; tag must be set for these Events. Previously, these Events were not duplicated to a new contract if they were in the "Waiting" status in the process of reissuing. Now the SKIP_FOR_DUPLICATE; tag must be set to avoid duplication of these Events. Otherwise, the Events will be duplicated to a new contract irrespective of the "Waiting" status, and the new contract may be closed, or other unwanted consequences may occur.
Updated Manuals: [product_management\Events.pdf]

Changed the behaviour of Event closure when a card is reissued for Event types that have "MOVE_FOR_DUPLICATE" or "CLOSE_FOR_DUPLICATE" tag in special parameters. If an Event type has both parameters Single Duration and Next Event, then Next Event will not be posted after the original Event has been closed. Previously it was posted.
Upgrade Note:
To search for problem Event types, run the check script CARDS-59029_DUPL_EVNT_01.sql
Check Scripts:
CARDS-59029_DUPL_EVNT_01.sql

WM-3296

Changed digital signature algorithm to SHA-512 for WAY4 Remote Access distributives (new installations and updates).
Upgrade Note:
To switch to the SHA-512 algorithm, reissue and reinstall the server application and all client applications.
To ensure operation is not interrupted during upgrade, it is recommended to do the following:
- For applications that have already been configured, issue a new update after WAY4 Cards has been updated.
- To gradually switch to the new algorithm for applications that have already been configured and new client applications, create a new application (Add new Application...) and new node (Nodes->Add...) with its own URL (internet_url). Export and install the new server application. Export and distribute the new client application for installation.
- After all client applications have been reinstalled, the old application with an old node can be deleted.

Reversal management

CARDS-59886

Added the ability to automatically post adjustment documents using backdated processing if a document's posting date is not specified. If the value of the global parameter USE_AUTO_STORNO is "J" or "Y", an adjustment document will be automatically posted using the original document's posting date, meaning both Advice and reversal macrotransactions will be backdated. Previously, if posting date was not specified, an Advice macrotransaction was posted with the current date.
Upgrade Note:
Changed behavior of automatic backdated processing when the value of the global parameter USE_AUTO_STORNO is "Y" . If no posting date is specified when posting an adjustment document, the date will be taken from the original document in the chain. An Advice macrotransaction will be posted with the date of the original document in the chain. Previously, Advice macrotransactions were posted with the current date.
Updated Manuals: [reversal_management\Reversal_Management.pdf]

CARDS-58556 / I1807084877

Added a check that CDU was performed for the contract involved in the backdated processing actions.
Upgrade Note:
Now if CDU for a contract has not been finished yet and the intelligent backdated processing is called for this contract (manual storno, previous cycle transaction conversion to instalment, etc.), the corresponding error is returned to ensure data consistency.
To finish CDU for this particular contract in the described situation and then to apply the Intelligent Backdated Processing action, the global parameter FORCE_CDU=Y must be set.
Updated Manuals: [reversal_management\Reversal_Management.pdf]

CARDS-55984

Changed codes and functional logic for the "Re-classify Card Products with DWD_CARD_CATEGORY" and "Re-classify Card Products with DWD_CARD_BRAND (OLD)" menu items from the file <OW_HOME>\opt\stat_reporting\client\dbm\menu\Card_Products_mapping_for_stat_reporting.UPG. Now these menu items use standard algorithm for Product mapping that is described in the dwh_mapping package.
Upgrade Note:
If the "Re-classify Card Products with DWD_CARD_CATEGORY" and "Re-classify Card Products with DWD_CARD_BRAND (OLD)" menu items are used during Product mapping for further statistics gathering in WAY4 Cards, it is strongly recommended to re-import the file <OW_HOME>\opt\stat_reporting\client\dbm\menu\Card_Products_mapping_for_stat_reporting.UPG and use new menu items that are created with the following codes:

OWSA.Re-Classify Card Products with DWD_CARD_CATEGORY)

Outdated logic for mapping Products using the dwd_card_brand and dwd_card_category classifiers has been changed in the opt_classify package. The own opt_classify logic was replaced by the calls of standard functions CLASSIFY_DWD_CARD_BRAND_IN and CLASSIFY_CARD_CATEGORY_IN from the dwh_mapping package. 
It is necessary to check the opt_classify.classify_dwd_card_brand and opt_classify.classify_dwd_card_category functions from the opt_classify package: 
- If these functions were not customised, according to the new standard version of opt_classify replace the opt_classify.classify_dwd_card_brand and opt_classify.classify_dwd_card_category functions with the dwh_mapping.CLASSIFY_DWD_CARD_BRAND_IN and dwh_mapping.CLASSIFY_CARD_CATEGORY_IN standard functions, respectively. 
- If these functions were customised, merge dwh_mapping.CLASSIFY_DWD_CARD_BRAND_IN and dwh_mapping.CLASSIFY_CARD_CATEGORY_IN with opt_classify.CLASSIFY_DWD_CARD_BRAND and opt_classify.CLASSIFY_CARD_CATEGORY and make the necessary changes in opt_classify.

In the "XLS_Visa_Statistics_Acquiring_Business" report, the P_IPS_REGION=VISA_CEMEA parameter must be used instead of obsolete parameter P_CEMEA=Y and the P_IPS_REGION=VISA_EUROPE parameter must be used instead of obsolete parameter P_CEMEA=N.
Updated Manuals: [visa_statistical_reports\quarterly_operating_certificates\VISA_Statistical_Reports.pdf]

CARDS-57970

Added a new parameter P_PAYMENT_SCHEME (varchar2(255), default value is "W") for the "XLS_NSPK_Statistics_Acquiring_Business" and "XLS_NSPK_Statistics_Acquiring_Devices" reports.
The parameter defines payment schemes which should be present in the report.
Upgrade Note:
The default payment scheme MP_PS_MEMBER.PAYMENT_SCHEME for which the "XLS_NSPK_Statistics_Acquiring_Business" and "XLS_NSPK_Statistics_Acquiring_Devices" reports are generated has been changed. To return to the old report behaviour, specify all payment schemes MP_PS_MEMBER.PAYMENT_SCHEME for which the report was generated earlier in the P_PAYMENT_SCHEME parameter.
Updated Manuals: NSPK Interface | MIR Statistical Reports

Added a new parameter P_ADDRESS_LINE for the "XLS_Visa_Statistics_Acquiring_Business" report (varchar2(255), default value is "to_char(c.billing_contract) || ad.address_line_1") for customising calculation of merchant outlets.
Upgrade Note:
To return the old report behaviour, set the P_ADDRESS_LINE parameter to "ad.address_line_1". In this case, for two merchants who have the same address, the number of merchant outlets is calculated as 1.

SYSTEM-515

Tariff management

CARDS-56728

Added a new check for the uniqueness of the "Tariff Code Ext" field (tariff.TABLE_CODE_FROM) in a personal domain when approving a personal tariff. If several tariffs with the same "Tariff Code Ext" are found in the same personal tariff domain, an error message with the text "There is more than one tariff with TariffCodeExt = %%" will be returned.
Upgrade Note:
The system configuration must be checked using preliminary script for the presence of a non-unique value for the tariff.TABLE_CODE_FROM (Tariff Code Ext) field in the tariff domain. If this is the case, the codes must be given unique values.
Check Scripts:
CARDS-56728_TARIFF_table_code_from_uniqueness.sql
Updated Manuals: [tariff_management\Tariff_Management.pdf]

CARDS-60170

Improved the Tariff Management product, added a separate "Priority" field to the tariff table instead of the "PRIOR" tag.
Upgrade Note:
The value of the "PRIOR" tag will be moved to a separate "Priority" field of the tariff table. If the tag is missing, "0" will be specified in the field.
The upgrade wizard will run a process called "Migrate Priority field for tariffs" and will update each active record in the TARIFF table. This process can be run in parallel mode if the PARALLEL parameter is configured for the "Migrate Priority field for tariffs" process in the "Process Parameters" form (OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Main Tables\Process Parameters).
Updated Manuals: [tariff_management\Tariff_Management.pdf]

CARDS-60213

Fixed OVL_THRESHOLD tariff behaviour when a personal tariff is used for the top issuing contract with affiliated subcontracts.
Upgrade Note:
If OVL_THRESHOLD is defined as a personal tariff for the top contract in a hierarchy, it will be applied for all contracts downward, even those which are linked to the top contract with Affiliated/Only Reporting types of liability links.
To use a personal OVL_THRESHOLD for the top level contract only, without affecting the available amount of Affiliated/Only Reporting liability subcontracts, the value PERS_DOMAIN_LEVEL=CURRENT; should be defined in the "Search Rules" field for the OVL_THRESHOLD tariff type.
Updated Manuals: [issuing\user_manuals\Issuing_Module.pdf] [tariff_management\Tariff_Management.pdf]

Tokenization

CARDS-61276

Changed token life cycle management during plastic reissuing events: the identification type parameter FOR_DUPLICATE should be equal to "MOVE_WHEN_ACTIVATE" for MDES / VTS to generate a PAN Update message and equal to "DEACTIVATE" for MIR to generate a Token Deactivation message.
Upgrade Note:
Procedures for renewing tokenized cards have been changed.
These changes ensure that data for a reissued card is synchronised for payment tokens in the issuer's system and in the payment system's tokenization service.

For identification types ("Authentication Module -> Identification Types") that are used for MDES, VDEP and MIR tokens, check if the "FOR_DUPLICATE" parameter is present.

If the parameter is absent, it must be added: "Parm Type" = "String", "Is Global" = "Yes".
For MDES and VDEP token identification types, set the parameter's default value to "MOVE_WHEN_ACTIVATE".
For MIR identification types, the default value must be "DEACTIVATE".

If the required settings are not made, when a tokenized card is reissued, if the card number changed, the card's tokens data may not be sent to the the payment system's tokenization service, and it will not be possible to further use the token for payment transactions.
Updated Manuals: Issuing | Tokenization | MDES | Setup Issuing | Tokenization | VDEP | Setup

CARDS-65266 / OWS-14596

Supported VISA 18Q4 3.19 basic participation framework for enrolling issuers in the VTS.
Upgrade Note:
To support Account verification service request message with the PAN
during token provisioning for issuers who don't participate in detailed Visa Token Service integration parameter AUTH_REQ_USE_BASIC_TOKEN added. Parameter contains list with IPS which have to be supported. Default value is null.  The value of the parameter is as follows:  if the MDES functionality is implemented - VISA,  if VISA is implemented - MC, if the MDES and VTS functionality is implemented - blank. Similarly,  the parameter is populated for other IPS (Abbreviation: UPI,AMEX).
Is is necessary to add Additional online service with "TKN_ACTIVATION" code using form  "Additional Online Services " ("Full → Configuration Setup → Merchant Device Setup → Additional Online Services").
Updated Manuals: [core\Global_Parameters.pdf]

Transaction management

CARDS-59845

Deleted the global parameter CHECK_OUR_CARD_BIN. Behaviour introduced in version 03.46 will be used without any parameters. In document processing for our cards, a BIN record will be searched for based on document parameters if the target contract number differs from the target document number or if the document terminal category differs from the BIN table terminal category (to which the contract subtype is linked).
Upgrade Note:
The global parameter CHECK_OUR_CARD_BIN will be deleted automatically from the configuration, if it was present.
Updated Manuals: [core\Global_Parameters.pdf]

Changed the response code for processed reversals and adjustments if the financial institution is changed for the contract (ACCEPT_CHANGE_FI=R/Y modes). Previously documents were converted to advice with response code 96, now response code 102 is specified.
Upgrade Note:
Check document-based reports and file interfaces taking into account new RC=102.
Updated Manuals: [core\Global_Parameters.pdf]

CARDS-58520

Eliminated attempts to fill BIN record reference on document accept and other card related checks for non-card contracts. The target contract's contract category is now checked instead of the transaction type's contract category.
Upgrade Note:
AUTH_TYPE and PAN document tags are no longer filled for mVisa payments. If the AUTH_TYPE tag was used to identify mVisa payments in product settings (e.g. services or usages), other distinguishing characteristic should be chosen (e.g. the BAI tag) and corresponding settings should be changed.

CARDS-58531

Removed multiple error messages if the "Approve" or "Accept" actions are performed for a document when the source number is missing. No search will be made for transaction authorisations with the "Interbank" and "Settlement" transaction types even if the "Is Authorized" field in the transaction type setup is set to "Always" or "May Be".
Upgrade Note:
Check that the "Is Authorized" field for the "Interbank" and "Settlement" transaction types is set to "Never". Use a check script to determine whether there is a transaction type that must be reconfigured.
Check Scripts:
CARDS-58531_impersonal_authorized_transtypes.sql

CARDS-59342

Removed the transaction attribute NO_PIN and corresponding group transaction condition <<All Pin Bypass (Group)>>.
Upgrade Note:
Clients who used the group transaction condition <<All Pin Bypass (Group)>> in services, risk rules, etc. must replace it with the group transaction condition <<All Pin Offline Capable, not PBT (Group)>>.
Check Scripts:
If check script CHECK_v1_CARDS-59342_GTC_G_NO_PIN.sql logs table ids in process "Check for presence obsolete Group Transaction Condition <<All Pin Bypass (Group)>>" you must replace there (after upgrade) group transaction condition <<All Pin Bypass (Group)>> (code G_NO_PIN) with the group transaction condition <<All Pin Offline Capable, not PBT (Group)>>.

CARDS-59489

Corrected fee amount calculation that was using the mtr.CRE_TEST_MTR procedure to work on secondary nodes of a high availability configuration.
Upgrade Note:
The procedure mtr.CRE_TEST_MTR will not raise an exception when executed on a secondary node of a high availability configuration. Custom code should be checked so that macrotransactions returned by the CRE_TEST_MTR procedure are not inserted into the database.

CARDS-62947

Created a check script to assess the impact on default system behaviour by changes in the calculation of a parent usage limiter's "Current Amount" field when the child limiter has the BASE_AMOUNT_TYPE tag.
Upgrade Note:
In the scope of product development in future versions, it is planned to change the algorithm for calculating the amount which is stored in a parent usage limiter's "Current Amount" field if the BASE_AMOUNT_TYPE tag is specified in the child usage limiter (the tag determines which amount from the document to consider in the limiter's counter in the "Current Amount" field). In current versions, the document amount is considered in the parent usage limiter counter, instead of the amount calculated and stored in the child usage limiter's "Current Amount" field. The new system behaviour will consider the same amount in the parent limiter as in the child limiter's "Current Amount" field.
To determine the new behaviour's impact on the existing system configuration, run the check script CARDS-62947_usg_lim_hierarchy.sql. If the script returns a result that is not empty, contact OpenWay Support and provide the script result data and a description of the business task for which this parent-child limiter pair is used.
Check Scripts:
CARDS-62947_usg_lim_hierarchy.sql

Updated Manuals: [ips_releases\visa\20XX_XX_VISA_Requirements.pdf]

CARDS-60304

Supported new processing rules for transactions with deferred authorization in VISA and Affiliated BASE II inward and outward pipes. 
The new message reason code value of 5206 (Deferred authorization) will be saved to the VISA_MRC tag on posting or inward processing. The transaction attribute DEFERRED will be set for such financial documents too. 
Pipes affected:
Affiliated BASEII Outward Processing.dll, Affiliated BASEII Prepared Outward Processing.dll, Visa Base II Outward Processing.dll, VISA BASEII ONUS Marked Outward Processing.dll, VISA BASEII ONUS Outward Processing.dll, VISA BASEII Prepared Outward Processing.dll.
VISA BASEII Inward Processing.dll, Affiliated VISA BASEII Inward Processing.dll

Packages affected:
stl_b.sql
tr_cond_b.sql

Procedure affected:
cust_mark_onus.sql
Upgrade Note:
Changed the format of returned values in the functions tr_cond.get_visa_ta and get_visa_ta_f. Now these functions return a tagged string, VISA_TA=<value>; the tag VISA_MRC=5206 is added at the end for deferred documents.
Due to the change in the format of returned values in these functions, the cust_mark_onus function code has changed. 
Required settings to activate this behaviour are described in the 2019_04_VISA_Requirements.pdf standard manual.
Updated Manuals: [ips_releases\visa\20XX_XX_VISA_Requirements.pdf]

CARDS-60588

Supported changes to Visa systems for migrating to eight-digit Issuing BINs in VISA BASEII Inward and Outward processing pipes pursuant to the VISA release requirement 4.7 Apr19-354. VISA Dialect changed.
Retired the Issuer RFC Sub-Address field, renamed the Issuer RFC BIN field.
Pipes affected:
Affiliated BASEII Inward Processing.dll
Affiliated BASEII Outward Processing.dll

VISA BASEII ONUS Outward Processing.dll

VISA FRS Outward Processing.dll
VISA NMAS Outward Processing.dll
Upgrade Note:
Settings required to activate this behaviour are described in the 2019_04_VISA_Requirements.pdf standard manual.
Updated Manuals: [ips_releases\visa\20XX_XX_VISA_Requirements.pdf]

WS Runtime

WSRT-273

Added a new field to the <ResultInfo> tag, "is_primary_available". This field's value is "Y" or "N" and indicates availability of the Primary Node in Distributed Processing architecture.
Upgrade Note:
In Distributed Processing mode, the protocol between front and worker WS Runtime nodes has changed without backward incompatibility. All front and worker WS Runtime nodes must be shut down before upgrade and be upgraded simultaneously.

Web services

WSRT-256

Added a type validation parameter (validate_requests_internally) for web services input parameters. It is turned on by default.
Upgrade Note:
Some web service input parameters are now validated more thoroughly (e.g. parameter length is checked where it was not checked previously). If this causes failures, set the attribute validate_requests_internally="no" in the options tag in global-options.xml.

    • [CARDS-65146]
      • Fixed incorrect MTP calculation with the BT_SIMPLE algorithm when the PAST_DUE balance is more than the MTP_AGED_PART amount.
      Upgrade Note:
      1. The script CARDS--65146_BALANCE_TYPE.sql checks a configuration for a MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV balance, which is used to calculate the minimum payment (MTP) according to the BT_SIMPLE algorithm. If the script result is not empty - note that rules for calculating MTP according to the BT_SIMPLE-PAST_DUE[-OVL] formula have been changed.
Old behavior:
CurrentDue = rate*(MTP_AGED_PART-PAST_DUE[-OVL])+MTP_AGED_FULL
New Behavior:
CurrentDue = rate*(MTP_AGED_PART-PAST_DUE+MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV[-OVL])+MTP_AGED_FULL
The reason for the change is that a MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV balance is part of a PAST_DUE balance and the previous behavior was found to be incorrect.
If the MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV balance is used in the configuration, this balance's setup must be checked. This balance type should be defined for the account template that is specified as the Due Template for the account template with the MTP_AGED_FULL balance.
Example:
A line of accounts is configured in an Account Scheme:
Fee Current->Fee Grace->Fee Billed
A fee is included in MTP as 100%. The Fee Grace account should be marked with the MTP_AGED_FULL balance. The Fee Billed account template must be marked with the MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV balance.
2. The script CARDS--65146_ACC_SCHEMES.sql checks the configuration for the mode for calculating MTP according to BT_SIMPLE-PAST_DUE [-OVL]. If this mode is used and there are also account templates marked with the MTP_AGED_FULL balance (i.e. included in MTP as 100%), it is recommended to switch to the new mode for calculation according to the following formula:
CurrentDue = rate*(MTP_AGED_PART-PAST_DUE+MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV-[OVL])+MTP_AGED_FULL
where MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV is the balance that was already (in previous cycles) included in MTP as 100% according to the MTP_AGED_FULL balance but has not been paid yet.
The following changes should be made to the configuration:
1) Create a new balance type MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV in the form "OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Accounting Setup\Balance Types" with the parameters:
Code = MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV
Main Only=Main Only
History Mode = None
2) For account templates which are defined as Due templates for the account templates marked with MTP_AGED_FULL balance - add the value MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV to the Extra Bal Type field.
Example:
The following account templates and ageing rule for them are defined in the account scheme:
Fee Current->Fee Grace->Fee Billed
The fee is included in MTP as 100%. In the current configuration, the Fee Grace account template is marked with the MTP_AGED_FULL balance. The Fee Billed account template is not marked with the MTP_AGED_FULL balance. In this case, this account template should be marked with MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV balance.
3) Recalculate the MTP_AGED_FULL_PREV balance for existing contracts by using "OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Accounting Setup\Balance Types"->Recalc Balance For All Contracts.
      Check Scripts:
      CARDS--65146_BALANCE_TYPE.sql
CARDS--65146_ACC_SCHEMES.sql
